excalidraw-plugin: parsed
tags: [excalidraw]

==⚠  Switch to EXCALIDRAW VIEW in the MORE OPTIONS menu of this document. ⚠==


# Text Elements
Madd ^Vh6NooVI

Natural Madd ^LywLTk3w

Secondary Madd ^J9aoxa1z

Linking Madd ^3aXsXyZJ

Madd lazem ^zwDRUkZl

Temporary Madd ^YZXwoqin

Eased Madd ^rmY2PcSH

The letters of natural madd are: ^IhSHOPWo

Madd are proceeded by short vowels (Fatha, Damma, Kasra)
Madd extend the word for 2 harakat (1 second) ^o9PMk3ka

Natural Madd letters have smaller version:  ^aaHyL11r

Connected Madd ^P6zi2EpR

Disconnected Madd ^D6Je1JwF

When the Madd is in the middle of the word (beginning or end doesn't count), 
you must extend for 5 Harakat (or 2.5 second) ^YCdG80ZB

When the Madd is at the end of the word
then you can optionally extend for 5harakat
(if you opt for not extending for 5 harakat
then you still have to extend for 2 harakat) ^Xb4t85tn

%%
